Jamison Brereton

15 (841)
Pitars
┼Ъaс╣Еkha Y─Бm─Бyana
14 verses: triс╣гс╣нubh, except jagat─л 11
This hymn is simply an expansion on the invitation in the last hymn (X.14.4тАУ6) to the forefathers to come to our sacrifice. They are repeatedly urged to sit on the ritual grass, to partake of the offerings, including soma, and to provide us with material and spiritual benefits in return. The language is quite straightforward, with very few verbal tricks. Only in verse 3 do we encounter a turn of phrase that invites our inquiry: in the first half of the verse тАЬIтАЭ find not only the forefathers on the ritual ground but also тАЬthe grandson/childтАЭ (n├бp─Бt) and the тАЬstride of Viс╣гс╣Зu.тАЭ The тАЬgrandsonтАЭ may be a reference to Agni, often called тАЬchild of strengthтАЭ (┼л╠Бrjo n├бp─Бt) and also frequently identified with the тАЬChild of the WatersтАЭ (Ap─Бm Nap─Бt), but it may also and simultaneously refer to the various descendants of the returning forefathers, descendants who would be present at the ritual and serving at it. As for Viс╣гс╣ЗuтАЩs wide stride, most commentators take this as the highest heaven, that is, the last of Viс╣гс╣ЗuтАЩs three strides. But it is hard to understand how this would be found тАЬhereтАЭ; we think rather that it refers to Viс╣гс╣ЗuтАЩs first stride, which measures out the earth, and in this case that it is a specific reference to the delineated sacrificial space.
Toward the end of the hymn, the god Agni becomes prominent (vss. 9тАУ14) and his special relationship with the forefathersтАФas their cremation fireтАФis alluded to (esp. vss. 11, 14).

010-019 ...{Loading}...
Jamison Brereton

The next ten hymns (X.10тАУ19) form a Yama cycle, though the subject matter found in the individual hymns is quite various. Yama, the son of Vivasvant, is king of the land of the dead because he was the first mortal to die. Yet he was apparently born immortal (see esp. I.83.5) and chose to become mortal, subject to death, тАЬfor the sake of the gods…and for the sake of offspringтАЭ (X.13.4). The opening hymn in the cycle, the dialogue of Yama and his twin sister Yam─л, on the fraught topic of embarking on incestuous sex in order to produce offspring, addresses YamaтАЩs change of status and his choice, but in a deliberately oblique and misleading fashion, as Yama spurns the sexual advances of his sister, and at the end of their bitter argument there seems little likelihood of children. The last six hymns in this cycle (X.14тАУ19) are collectively known as funeral hymns. The first, X.14, is devoted especially to Yama in his role as king of the realm of the dead, while the others, especially 15тАУ18, concern various aspects of death and the treatment of the deadтАФfor example, the forefathers who preceded us to YamaтАЩs realm in X.15, the cremation fire in X.16, the funeral itself in X.

The intermediate hymns, X.11тАУ13, have less superficially clear connections to the Yama saga, but both X.12 (vss. 6тАУ7) and X.13 (vss. 4тАУ5) make important comments on Yama and on YamaтАЩs choice.

There is also an underlying unifying theme, that of duality and twinned-ness: the absolute disjunction between and the ultimate complementarity and unity of the mortal and the immortal, life and death, men and gods, men and women, heaven and earth, sacred and profane. It is appropriate that the cycle should begin with the dialogue between the primal twins, Yama and Yam─л, whose very names mean тАЬtwinтАЭ and who bridge the gap between mortal and immortal.

тАЬLet the lower, the upper, the intermediate Pitс╣Ыs, rise up, accepting the Soma libation; may thoseprogenitors who, unlike wolves, acknowledging our offerings, have come to preserve our lives, protect us uponour invocations.тАЭ

Let the nearer ones rise up, up the further, up those in the middleтАФthe forefathers deserving of soma.
Those who have gone to (their next) life avoiding the wolf, knowing the truth, let those forefathers help us at the invocations.

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬLet this our adoration be today addressed to those Pitс╣Ыs our predecessors, to those our successors,who have departed (to the world of the manes); to those who are seated in the terrestrial sphere, to those whoare present among opulent people.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

Our successors: p┼лrv─Бsaс╕е = elder brother, father, grandfather, and thelike, born before the birth of the worshipper; upar─Бsaс╕е means younger brothers, sons, etc. ; or, those who havegone to svarga; upar─Бsaс╕е, those who have ceased or rested, who have gone to the world of brahm─Б (Yajuс╣г19.68); in the terrestrial sphere: p─Бrthive rajasi = pс╣Ыthiv─лsambandhini rajo guс╣Зak─Бryesmin karmaс╣Зi, at thisritw which is connected with the earth is the effect of (or has for its effect) the quality of rajas (passion, or theactive principle);

Rajas = jyotiс╣г, light– terrestrial light or fire– the phrase no doubt refers to the fire altar (Yajuс╣г19.68)

Jamison Brereton

Let this homage here today be for the forefathersтАФthose who went previously, those who went later,
those who are seated here in the earthly realm, or who are now among the clans of good community.

Griffith

Now let us pay this homage to the Fathers, to those who passed of old and those who followed,
Those who have rested in the earthly region, and those who dwell among the Mighty Races.

Geldner

Diese Verbeugung soll heute den V├дtern gelten, die fr├╝her und die sp├дter gegangen sind, die sich in der irdischen Welt niedergesetzt haben, oder die jetzt bei verb├╝ndeten Clanen sind.

Grassmann

Dies Andachtswerk sei heut geweiht den V├дtern, die fr├╝her und die sp├дter heimgegangen, Die in der Luft, der Erde wohnen, oder in sch├╢nbewohnten D├╢rfern nun verweilen.

Elizarenkova

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬI have brought to my presence the Pitс╣Ыs who are well cognizant (of my worship), the infallibility, andfood of the effused (Soma) with the sacrificial cake.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

The infallibility…sacrifice: nap─Бtam, vikramaс╣Зam = paths ofthe gods, whence there is no falling and where there is going and coming– both as the consequence of sacrifice(Yajus. 29.56)

Jamison Brereton

I have found here the forefathers good to find and the grandson and the wide stride of Viс╣гс╣Зu.
Those who, sitting on the ritual grass, share in the pressed soma and the food at (the cry of) тАЬsvadh─Б,тАЭ they are the most welcome arrivals here.

1 have attained the gracious-minded Fathers, I have gained son and progeny from Visnu.
They who enjoy pressed juices with oblation seated on sacred grass, come oftenest hither.

рд╣реЗ рдмрд░реНрд╣рд┐рд╖рджрдГ ред рдпрдЬреНрдЮреЗ рд╕реАрджрдиреНрддреАрддрд┐ рдмрд░реНрд╣рд┐рд╖рджрдГ ред рдЕрддреНрд░рд╛рдкрд┐ тАШ рдпреЗ рд╡реИ рдпрдЬреНрд╡рд╛рдирд╕реНрддреЗ рдкрд┐рддрд░реЛ рдмрд░реНрд╣рд┐рд╖рджрдГ’ (рддреИ.рдмреНрд░рд╛.рез.рем.реп) рдЗрддреНрдпрддреНрд░ рд╢реНрд░реБрддрддреНрд╡рд╛рджреНрдпрд╛рдЧрдВ рдХреГрддреНрд╡рд╛ рдкреНрд░реЗрддреНрдп рдкрд┐рддреГрд▓реЛрдХрдВ рдкреНрд░рд╛рдкреНрддрд╛ рдмрд░реНрд╣рд┐рд╖рджрдГ ред рддрд╛рджреГрд╢рд╛ рд╣реЗ рдкрд┐рддрд░рдГ рдЕрд░реНрд╡рд╛рдХреН рдЕрд░реНрд╡рд╛рдЪреАрдирд╛рдирд╛рдорд╕реНрдорд╛рдХрдореН рдКрддреА рд░рдХреНрд╖рд╛ рднрд╡рджреНрднрд┐рдГ рдХрд░реНрддрд╡реНрдпреЗрддрд┐ рд╢реЗрд╖рдГ ред рд╡рдГ рдпреБрд╖реНрдорджрд░реНрдердореН рдЗрдорд╛ рд╣рд╡реНрдпрд╛ рдПрддрд╛рдирд┐ рд╣рд╡реАрдВрд╖рд┐ рдЪрдХреГрдо рдЕрддрд╕реНрддрд╛рдирд┐ рдЬреБрд╖рдзреНрд╡рдореН ред рддреЗ рд╣рд╡рд┐рд░реНрдЬреБрд╖реНрдЯрд╡рдиреНрддреЛ рдпреВрдпрдВ рд╢рдВрддрдореЗрди рд╕реБрдЦрддрдореЗрди рдЕрд╡рд╕рд╛ рд░рдХреНрд╖рдгреЗрди рдирд┐рдорд┐рддреНрддрднреВрддреЗрди рдЖ рдЧрдд рдЖрднрд┐рдореБрдЦреНрдпреЗрдирд╛рд╕реНрдорд╛рдиреН рдкреНрд░рд╛рдкреНрдиреБрдд ред рдЕрде рдЕрдирдиреНрддрд░рдВ рдирдГ рдЕрд╕реНрдорднреНрдпрдВ рд╢рдВ рд╕реБрдЦрдВ рдпреЛрдГ рджреБрдГрдЦрд╡рд┐рдпреЛрдЧрдореН рдЕрд░рдкрдГ рдкрд╛рдкрд░рд╣рд┐рддрдВ рдЪ рджрдзрд╛рдд рджрддреНрдд рее

рднрдЯреНрдЯрднрд╛рд╕реНрдХрд░-рдЯреАрдХрд╛

6рдЖрдордиреНрддреНрд░реНрдпрдиреНрддреЗ - рд╣реЗ рдмрд░реНрд╣рд┐рд╖рджрдГ рдкрд┐рддрд░рдГ рдКрддреА рдКрддреНрдпрд╛ рдЧрдордиреЗрди рдЕрд░реНрд╡рд╛рдХреН рдЕрд╕реНрдорд╛рдиреН рдкреНрд░рддреНрдпрднрд┐рдореБрдЦрд╛ рднреВрддреНрд╡рд╛ ред ‘рдКрддрд┐рдпреВрддрд┐’ рдЗрддреНрдпрд╛рджрд┐рдирд╛ рдЙрджрд╛рддреНрддрдГ рдХреНрддрд┐рдиреНрдирд┐рдкрд╛рддрд┐рддрдГ, ‘рд╕реБрдкрд╛рдВ рд╕реБрд▓реБрдХреН’ рдЗрддрд┐ рддреГрддреАрдпрд╛рдпрд╛рдГ рдкреВрд░реНрд╡рд╕рд╡рд░реНрдгрдГ, ‘рдЙрджрд╛рддреНрддрд╕реНрд╡рд░рд┐рддрдпреЛрд░реНрдпрдгрдГ’ рдЗрддрд┐ рддрддрдГрдкрд░рд╕реНрдпрд╛рдХрд╛рд░рд╕реНрдп рд╕рдВрд╣рд┐рддрд╛рдпрд╛рдВ рд╕реНрд╡рд░рд┐рддрддреНрд╡рдореН ред
рдЗрдорд╛рдирд┐ рд╣рд╡реНрдпрд╛рдирд┐ рд╣рд╡реАрдВрд╖рд┐ ред рдЙрднрдпрддреНрд░ ‘рд╢реЗрд╢реНрдЫрдиреНрджрд╕рд┐’ рдЗрддрд┐ рд▓реЛрдкрдГ ред

English translation:

тАЬPitс╣Ыs, Barhiс╣гads, protect (us who are) in your presence; we have made these oblations for you,accept them; come with your most felicitous protection, and bestow upon us health and happiness; and pardonfrom sin.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

With your most felicitous protection: avas─Б ┼Ыantamena = satisfied by most excellent food

Jamison Brereton

You forefathers who sit on the ritual grass inclined this way with your aid, we have made these oblations for you. Enjoy!
Come here with your most luck-bringing help. Then provide for us luck and lifetime without flaw.

Griffith

Fathers who sit on sacred grass, come, help us: these offerings have we made for you; accept them.
So come to us with most auspicious favour, and give us health and strength without a trouble.

рдкрджрд╛рд░реНрдерд╛рдиреНрд╡рдпрднрд╛рд╖рд╛рдГ - (рдмрд░реНрд╣рд┐рд╖рджрдГ рдкрд┐рддрд░рдГ рдКрддреА-рдЕрд░реНрд╡рд╛рдХреН-рд╡рдГ-рдЗрдорд╛ рд╣рд╡реНрдпрд╛-рдЪрдХреГрдо рдЬреБрд╖рдзреНрд╡рдореН) рдпрдЬреНрдЮрд╛рд╕рди рдЙрдкрд╡рд┐рд╖реНрдЯрд╛ рдКрддреА-рдКрддреНрдпреИ-рдЕрд╕реНрдорджреНрд░рдХреНрд╖рд╛рдпреИ тАЬрд╕реБрдкрд╛рдВ рд╕реБрдкреЛ рднрд╡рдиреНрддрд┐тАЭ [рдЕрд╖реНрдЯрд╛режренредрезредрейреп рд╡рд╛рд░реНрддрд┐рдХрдореН] рд╡рд┐рднрдХреНрддрд┐рд╡реНрдпрддреНрдпрдпрдГред рдЕрддреНрд░ рдпрдЬреНрдЮреЗ рдпреБрд╖реНрдорднреНрдпрдорд┐рдорд╛рдирд┐ рд╣рд╡реНрдпрд╛рдирд┐ рдХреБрд░реНрдордГ рд╕рдореНрдкрд╛рджрдпрд╛рдордГ рд╕рдЬреНрдЬреАрдХреБрд░реНрдореЛ рдпреВрдпрдВ рдЬреБрд╖рдзреНрд╡рдордЧреНрдиреМ рдкреНрд░рдХреНрд╖реЗрдкрд╛рд░реНрдердВ рдкреНрд░рдпреБрдЩреНрдзреНрд╡рдореН (рддреЗ рд╢рдВрддрдореЗрди-рдЕрд╡рд╕рд╛-рдЖрдЧрдд рдирдГ рдЕрд░рдкрдГ рд╢рдВрдпреЛрдГ рджрдзрд╛рдд) рддреЗ рдпреВрдпрдВ рд╡рд┐рджреНрд╡рд╛рдВрд╕рдГ рд╕реБрдЦрдордпреЗрди рд░рдХреНрд╖рдгреЗрди рд╕рджреИрд╡ рдкреНрд░рд╛рдкреНрдиреБрдд, рдЕрд╕реНрдорднреНрдпрдВ рдкрд╛рдкрд░рд╣рд┐рддрдВ рднрд╛рд╡рдВ рд░реЛрдЧрд╛рдгрд╛рдВ рд╢рдордирдВ рдпрд╛рд╡рдирдВ рдЪ рднрдпрд╛рдирд╛рдВ рдзрд╛рд░рдпрдд, рддрдерд╛ рдЪ рдирд┐рд░реБрдХреНрддрдореН [рекредрезрез] реерекрее

English translation:

тАЬMay the Pitс╣Ыs who are entitled to the Soma come, when invoked by us, to the agreeable treasuresconnected with the sacred grass; let them here listen (to our praises), let them speak (their approbation in reply);let them protect us.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

Entitled to the Soma: somy─Бsaс╕е = anugraha par─Бс╕е, kind or favourable,somasamp─Бdinaс╕е, obtaining the Soma

Jamison Brereton

The forefathers deserving of soma have been summoned here to the dear stores on the ritual grass.
Let them come hither, let them listen (to us) here; let them speak on
(our) behalf, let them help us.1394 X.16

Griffith

May they, the Fathers, worthy of the Soma, invited to their favourite oblations.
Laid on the sacred grass, come nigh and listen: may they be gracious unto us and bless us.

Geladen sind die Soma-frohen V├дter zu lieben Speisen, welche auf der Streu stehn; Sie m├╢gen kommen und uns hier erh├╢ren und freundlich zu uns reden und uns helfen.

English translation:

тАЬHaving sat down on the right side withbended knee, do you all accept this sacrifice. Harm us notPitс╣Ыs, for any offence which through human (infirmity) we may have committed towards you.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

Having bent your knee, having sat down to the south, greet this sacrifice hereтАФall of you.
Do not harm us, o forefathers, because of any offense that we may do to you in our human way.

Griffith

Bowing your bended knees and seated southward, accept this sacrifice of ours with favour.
Punish us not for any sin, O Fathers, which we through human frailty have committed.

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬSeated in the proximity of the radiant (flames of the altar), bestow riches on the mortal donor (of theoblation); give wealth, Pitс╣Ыs, to his sons; do you who are present grant us vigour.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

In the proximity of the radiant:aruс╣З─лn─Бm upasthe, purple-coloured: applied to the wool of which the blanked called kuс╣нapu is made of whichPitс╣Ыs are fond, kutс╣нapapriyaс╕е pitara (Yajus. 19.63); give wealth to his sons: tasya yajam─Бnasya; bestow thiswealth on your sons

Jamison Brereton

Sitting in the lap of the ruddy (Dawns?), provide wealth for the pious mortal.
To your sons, o forefathers, hold out (a portion) of this good thing.
Provide nourishment here.

Griffith

Lapped in the bosom of the purple Mornings, give riches to the man who brings oblations.
Grant to your sons a portion of that treasure, and, present, give them energy, ye Fathers.

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬMay Yama, being propitiated, desirous (of the offering), partake at plural asure of the oblations along withthose our ancient progenitors of the Saumyas, the possessors of great wealth, who also desire it, and whoconveyed the Soma (to the gods and to the Pitс╣Ыs) in order.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

Our ancient progenitors: p┼лrve pitaraс╕е, who, asprogenitors when living, offered the Soma, and now, as Pitс╣Ыs, partake of it;

Vasiс╣гс╣нh─Бс╕е = vastс╣Ыtam─Бhkс╣Ыt─Бcch─Бdan─Б dhanavattam─Б v─Б, covering or most wealthy; or, of the race of Vasiс╣гс╣нha (Yajus. 19.51)

Jamison Brereton

Those ancient forefathers of ours deserving of soma, the Vasiс╣гс╣нhas, who journeyed along to the soma-drinking,
in joint enjoyment with them let YamaтАФhe eager with them eagerтАФeat the oblations according to their desire.

Griffith

Our ancient Fathers who deserve the Soma, who came, most noble, to our Soma banquet,-
With these let Yama, yearning with the yearning, rejoicing eat our offerings at his pleasure.

Geldner

Unsere somaw├╝rdigen Vorv├дter, die Vasistha┬┤s, die zum Somatrunk gefahren sind, mit denen soll Yama die Opfergaben gemeinsam und voll Verlangen mit den Verlangenden nach Wunsch genie├Яen.

Grassmann

Mit unsern Ahnen, die den Soma lieben, den besten, die zum Somatrunk gekommen, Geniesse Jama huldreich unsre Tr├дnke behaglich mit den gierigen begierig.

Elizarenkova

English translation:

тАЬCome, Agni, to our presence with the Pitс╣Ыs, who are possessed of knowledge, who having attained aseat among the gods, thirst (for the Soma), skilled in sacrifices, reciters of praises with hymns, truth-speaking,seers, frequenters of sacrifices.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

Those who have thirsted, panting, among the gods, those knowing the priestly functions, those fashioned by praise along with chantsтАФ
with them, o Agni, drive here, turned this wayтАФwith the forefathers who are good to find and truly here, the poets who sit by the gharma drink.

Griffith

Come to us, Agni, with the gracioug Fathers who dwell in glowing light, the very Kavyas,
Who thirsted mid the Gods, who hasten hither, oblation winners, theme of singers’ praises.

Geldner

Grassmann

Die bei den G├╢ttern sitzend, lechzend d├╝rsten, die Opfer kennend, mit Gesang gepriesen, Mit denen, Agni, komm, den holden V├дtern, den treuen, weisen, die im Lichte wohnen.

тАЬCome, Agni, with thousands of Pitс╣Ыs, of both past and future (time), frequenters of sacrifices, eulogistsof the gods; those who are true, who feed on oblations, and drink oblations, possessing equality with Indra andthe gods.тАЭ

тАЬAgniс╣гv─Бtta Pitс╣Ыs, come to this solemnity; sit down, directors in the right way, in your appropriateplaces; eat the oblations spread on the grass, and grant us riches and male posterity.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

Sweetened by Agni, o forefathers, come here. Sit each on his own seat, you of good guidance.
Eat the oblations set forth on the ritual grass. Then provide wealth in hale heroes.

Griffith

Fathers whom Agni’s flames have tasted, come ye nigh: ye kindly leaders, take ye each your proper place.
Eat sacrificial food presented on the grass: grant riches with a multitude of hero sons.

English translation:

тАЬAgni J─Бtavedas, who are glorified (by us), having made our oblations fragrant, you have borne themoff, and have presented them to the Pitс╣Ыs; may they partake of them with the Svadh─Б; and do you also, divineAgni, feed upon the offered oblations.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

Yajus. 19.66: j─Бtavedas = kavyav─Бhana; with the svadh─Б:svadh─Бk─Бreс╣Зa, i.e., with the exclamation, svadh─Б! or, it may mean, along with the svadh─Б or pitс╣Ы-oblationitself

Jamison Brereton

You, Agni J─Бtavedas, reverently invoked, have conveyed the oblations, having made them very fragrant.
You have presented them to the forefathers; they have eaten them at
(the cry of) тАЬsvadh─Б.тАЭ (Now) you, o godтАФeat the oblations set forth.

And give them to the Fathers who did cat them with Svadha. Eat, thou God, the gifts we bring thee.

English translation:

тАЬYou know, J─Бtavedas, those Pitс╣Ыs, how many they may be, who are not in this world, those whom weknow, and those whom we do not fully know; enjoy this pious sacrifice offered together with svadh─Бs.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

Both the forefathers who are here and those who are not here, both those whom we know and those whom we do not know,
you know how many they are, o J─Бtavedas. Through your own powers [/at svadh─Б-calls], enjoy the well-performed sacrifice.

Griffith

Thou, Jatavedas, knowest well the number of Fathers who are here and who are absent,
Of Fathers whom we know and whom we know not: accept the sacrifice wellprepared with portions.

рдпреЗ рдкрд┐рддрд░рдГ рдЕрдЧреНрдирд┐рджрдЧреНрдзрд╛рдГ рдЕрдЧреНрдирд┐рдирд╛ рднрд╕реНрдореАрдХреГрддрд╛рдГред рд╢реНрдорд╢рд╛рдирдВ рдкреНрд░рд╛рдкреНрддрд╛ рдЗрддреНрдпрд░реНрдердГ ред рдпреЗ рдЪ рдкрд┐рддрд░рдГ рдЕрдирдЧреНрдирд┐рджрдЧреНрдзрд╛рдГ рд╢реНрдорд╢рд╛рдирдХрд░реНрдо рди рдкреНрд░рд╛рдкреНрддрд╛рдГ рдордзреНрдпреЗ рджрд┐рд╡рдГ рджреНрдпреБрд▓реЛрдХрд╕реНрдп рдордзреНрдпреЗ рд╕реНрд╡рдзрдпрд╛ рд╣рд╡рд┐рд░реНрд▓рдХреНрд╖рдгреЗрдирд╛рдиреНрдиреЗрди рдорд╛рджрдпрдиреНрддреЗ рддреГрдкреНрдпрдиреНрддрд┐’ рд╣реЗ рдЕрдЧреНрдиреЗ рд╕реНрд╡рд░рд╛рдЯреН рд╕реНрд╡рдХрд░реНрдореЛрдкрднреЛрдЧреЗрди рджреАрдкреНрдпрдорд╛рдирдГ рддреЗрднрд┐рдГ рддреИрдГ рдкрд┐рддреГрднрд┐рдГ рд╕рд╣рд┐рддрдГ рд╕рдиреН рдЕрд╕реБрдиреАрддрд┐рдВ рдкреНрд░рд╛рдгрд╛рдирд╛рдВ рд╡рд┐рд╖рдпреЗрд╖реБ рдиреЗрддрд╛рд░рдорд╕реНрдорддреНрдкрд┐рддреНрд░рдиреНрддрд░рд╛рддреНрдорд╛рдирдореН рдПрддрд╛рдВ рддрдиреНрд╡рдореН рдПрддрджреНрджреЗрд╡рддрд╛рд╢рд░реАрд░рдВ рдпрдерд╛рд╡рд╢рдВ рдпрдерд╛рдХрд╛рдордВ рдХрд▓реНрдкрдпрд╕реНрд╡ рд╕рдорд░реНрдердпрд╕реНрд╡ ред рдЧреНрд░рд╛рд╕рдпреЗрддреНрдпрд░реНрдердГрее рее резреп рее

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬMay those who are agnidagdhas, and those who are not, be satisfied with svadh─Б in the midst ofheaven; and do you supreme lord, associated with them, construct at your plural asure that body that is endowedwith breath.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

Agnidagdhas: those whose bodies have been burnt by the obsequial fire; supreme lord: svar─Бt. =Agni; or Yama (Yajus. 19.60); asun─лtim tanvam = the body that leads to life– a divine body; or long-lived

Jamison Brereton

Those burned by fire and those not burned by fire who become
exhilarated at (the cry of) тАЬsvadh─БтАЭ in the middle of heaven,
along with them (go) as sovereign king (on the way) leading to (the
other) life. Arrange your body as you wish.

Griffith

They who, consumed by fire or not cremated, joy in their offering in the midst of heaven,-
Grant them, O Sovran Lord, the world of spirits and their own body, as thy pleasure wills it.

Geldner

Die im Feuer verbrannt und nicht im Feuer verbrannt, in der Mitte des Himmels sich der Geisterspeise erfreuen, mit denen geh als freier Herr diesen Weg ins Jenseits! Nimm nach Wunsch einen neuen Leib an!

Grassmann

Mit den verbrannten und den nicht verbrannten, die lustig schwelgen in des Himmels Mitte, Mit denen f├╝hr, o Herrscher, diesen K├╢rper zum Geisterreich und bild’ ihn nach Gefallen.

рдЕрдзрд┐рдордиреНрддреНрд░рдореН (VC)

  • рд╢рдЩреНрдЦреЛ рдпрд╛рдорд╛рдпрдирдГ
  • рд╡рд┐рд░рд╛рдЯреНрддреНрд░рд┐рд╖реНрдЯреБрдкреН
  • рдзреИрд╡рддрдГ
рдмреНрд░рд╣реНрдордореБрдирд┐ - рдкрджрд╛рд░реНрдердГ

рдкрджрд╛рд░реНрдерд╛рдиреНрд╡рдпрднрд╛рд╖рд╛рдГ - (рдпреЗ-рдЕрдЧреНрдирд┐рджрдЧреНрдзрд╛рдГ-рдпреЗ рдЕрдирдЧреНрдирд┐рджрдЧреНрдзрд╛рдГ-рджрд┐рд╡рдГ рдордзреНрдпреЗ рд╕реНрд╡рдзрдпрд╛ рдорд╛рджрдпрдиреНрддреЗ) рдЕрдЧреНрдирд┐рддреЗрдЬ рдпрд╛ рддрд╛рдк рдЬрд┐рди рдХрд┐рд░рдгреЛрдВ рд╕реЗ рдмреЭ рдЬрд╛рддрд╛ рд╣реИ, рд╡реЗ рдЧреНрд░реАрд╖реНрдордХрд╛рд▓ рдЕрд░реНрдерд╛рддреН рдЙрддреНрддрд░рд╛рдпрдг рдХреЗ рдЕрдиреНрдд рдХреА рддрдерд╛ рдЙрдирд╕реЗ рд╡рд┐рдкрд░реАрдд рд╢реАрддрдХрд╛рд▓ рдЕрд░реНрдерд╛рддреН рджрдХреНрд╖рд┐рдгрд╛рдпрди рдХреЗ рдЕрдиреНрдд рдХреА рд╕реВрд░реНрдпрд░рд╢реНрдорд┐рдпрд╛рдБ, рдЬреЛ рдЖрдХрд╛рд╢ рдХреЗ рдордзреНрдп рдореЗрдВ рд╡рд┐рдЪрд░рддреА рд╣реБрдИ рдЬрд▓рд╡реГрд╖реНрдЯрд┐ рд╕реЗ рдкреНрд░рд╛рдгрд┐рдпреЛрдВ рдХреЛ рдЬреАрд╡рди рджреЗрддреА рд╣реИрдВ (рд╕реНрд╡рд░рд╛рдЯреН рддреЗрднрд┐рдГ-рдПрддрд╛рдореН-рдЕрд╕реБрдиреАрддрд┐рдВ рддрдиреНрд╡рдВ рдпрдерд╛рд╡рд╢рдВ рдХрд▓реНрдкрдпрд╕реНрд╡)рд╣реЗ рдпрдЬреНрдЮ рдореЗрдВ рдкреНрд░рдХрд╛рд╢рдорд╛рдирд╛рдЧреНрдиреЗ ! рдЙрди рдХрд┐рд░рдгреЛрдВ рдХреЗ рджреНрд╡рд╛рд░рд╛ рдкреНрд░рд╛рдгрд╕рдЮреНрдЪрд╛рд░ рдХреЗ рд╕реНрдерд╛рди рдЬреАрд╡рд╢рд░реАрд░ рдХреЛ рдпрдерд╛рдпреЛрдЧреНрдп рд╕рдорд░реНрде рдмрдирд╛ реерезрекрее

рдмреНрд░рд╣реНрдордореБрдирд┐ - рднрд╛рд╡рд╛рд░реНрдердГ

рднрд╛рд╡рд╛рд░реНрдерднрд╛рд╖рд╛рдГ - рдЙрддреНрддрд░рд╛рдпрдг рдФрд░ рджрдХреНрд╖рд┐рдгрд╛рдпрди рдХреЗ рдЕрдиреНрдд рдореЗрдВ рд╣реЛрдиреЗрд╡рд╛рд▓реА рд╡рд░реНрд╖рд╛ рдХреА рдХрд╛рд░рдгрднреВрдд рд╕реВрд░реНрдпрдХрд┐рд░рдгреЛрдВ рдХреЛ рдЖрдХрд╛рд╢ рд╕реЗ рд╕реБрд╡реГрд╖реНрдЯрд┐ рдХреЗ рд▓рд┐рдпреЗ рдпрдЬреНрдЮрд╛рдЧреНрдирд┐ рдкреНрд░реЗрд░рд┐рдд рдХрд░рддреА рд╣реИ, рдЬрд┐рд╕ рд╕реЗ рдЬреАрд╡рд╢рд░реАрд░ рдпрдерд╛рдпреЛрдЧреНрдп рдкреНрд░рд╛рдгрд╢рдХреНрддрд┐ рдХреЛ рдзрд╛рд░рдг рдХрд░ рд╕рдХрддрд╛ рд╣реИ реерезрекрее

рдмреНрд░рд╣реНрдордореБрдирд┐ - рдкрджрд╛рд░реНрдердГ

рдкрджрд╛рд░реНрдерд╛рдиреНрд╡рдпрднрд╛рд╖рд╛рдГ - (рдпреЗ рдЕрдЧреНрдирд┐рджрдЧреНрдзрд╛рдГ-рдпреЗ-рдЕрдирдЧреНрдирд┐рджрдЧреНрдзрд╛рдГ-рджрд┐рд╡рдГ-рдордзреНрдпреЗ рд╕реНрд╡рдзрдпрд╛ рдорд╛рджрдпрдиреНрддреЗ) рдпреЗ рдЕрдЧреНрдирд┐рджрдЧреНрдзрд╛рдГ рдЕрдЧреНрдирд┐рд░реНрджрдЧреНрдзреЛ рджреАрдкрд┐рддреЛ рдпреИрд╕реНрддреЗ рдЧреНрд░реИрд╖реНрдорд╛ рдЙрддреНрддрд░рд╛рдпрдгрд╛рдиреНрддреЗ рднрд╡рд╛рдГ рд╕реВрд░реНрдпрд░рд╢реНрдордпрдГ, тАЬрдЬрд╛рддрд┐рдХрд╛рд▓рд╕реБрдЦрд╛рджрд┐рднреНрдпреЛрд╜рдирд╛рдЪреНрдЫрд╛рджрдирд╛рддреН рдХреНрддреЛрд╜рдХреГрддрдорд┐рдд-рдкреНрд░рддрд┐рдкрдиреНрдирд╛рдГтАЭ [рдЕрд╖реНрдЯрд╛режремредреиредрезренреж] рдЗрддрд┐ рд╕реВрддреНрд░реЗрдг рдмрд╣реБрд╡реНрд░реАрд╣рд╛рд╡рдиреНрддреЛрджрд╛рддреНрддрдГ, рджрд╣ рдзрд╛рддреБрд░реНрджреАрдкреНрддреМ тАЬрджрд╣рд┐рдХреН рджреАрдкреНрддреМтАЭ [рдХрд╡рд┐рдХрд▓реНрдкрджреНрд░реБрдордГ] рдпреЗрд╜рдирдЧреНрдирд┐рджрдЧреНрдзрд╛рд╕реНрддрджреНрд╡рд┐рдкрд░реАрддрд╛ рд╣реИрдордиреНрддрд┐рдХрд╛ рджрдХреНрд╖рд┐рдгрд╛рдпрдирд╛рдиреНрддреЗ рднрд╡рд╛рдГ рд╕реВрд░реНрдпрд░рд╢реНрдордпрд╕реНрддреЗ рд╕рд░реНрд╡реЗ рджрд┐рд╡реЛрд╜рдиреНрддрд░рд┐рдХреНрд╖рд╕реНрдп рдордзреНрдпреЗ рд╕реНрд╡рдзрдпреЛрджрдХреЗрдиреЛрджрдХрд╡реГрд╖реНрдЯреНрдпрд╛ рдорд╛рджрдпрдиреНрддреЗ рдкреНрд░рд╛рдгрд┐рдиреЛ рдЬреАрд╡рдпрдиреНрддрд┐ (рд╕реНрд╡рд░рд╛рдЯреН рддреЗрднрд┐рдГ-рдПрддрд╛рдореН-рдЕрд╕реБрдиреАрддрд┐рдВ рддрдиреНрд╡рдВ рдпрдерд╛рд╡рд╢рдВ рдХрд▓реНрдкрдпрд╕реНрд╡) рд╕реНрд╡рд░рд╛рдЯреН-рд╣реЗ рдкреНрд░рдХрд╛рд╢рдорд╛рдирд╛рдЧреНрдиреЗ ! рддреЗрднрд┐рдГ рд╕реВрд░реНрдпрд░рд╢реНрдорд┐рднрд┐рд░реЗрддрд╛рдВ рддрдиреНрд╡рдореЗрддрдВ рдЬреАрд╡рд╢рд░реАрд░рдорд╕реБрдиреАрддрд┐рдВ рдкреНрд░рд╛рдгрд╕рдЮреНрдЪрд╛рд░рд╕реНрдерд╛рдирдВ рдпрдерд╛рд╡рд╢реНрдпрдХрдВ рдпрдерд╛рдпреЛрдЧреНрдпрдВ рд╕рдорд░реНрдердпрд╕реНрд╡ реерезрекрее
